<h2><a name="bookmark23"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark24"></a>Kadar Air</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">cara prage</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">latinisasi dan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rhadap kadar air biskuit. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 2 dapat dilihat bahwa kadar air biskuit be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 2,61% sampai de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan 3,52%. Kadar air te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P0 (100:0) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 2,61% yang tidak be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">da nyata de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P1 (90:10) dan P2 (80:20) yaitu masing-masing se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 2,75% dan 2,90%, se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">dangkan nilai kadar air te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P5 (50:50) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 3,52% yang tidak be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">da nyata de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P4 (60:40) yaitu 3,25%. Kadar air pada biskuit me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngalami ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">naikan se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">iring de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ningkatnya pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nambahan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah, hal ini kare</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">na kadar air yang ada dalam te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">bih be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar dibandingkan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 1 dapat dilihat bahwa kadar air te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 6,10% le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">bih re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah dibandingkan kadar air dalam te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 9,37%.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mampuan bahan pangan dalam me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngikat air juga tidak te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rle</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pas dari ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ikutse</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rtaan kandungan pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">innya. Hal ini juga didukung o</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h Agustina dan Fitriani (2021), yang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nyatakan bahwa kadar air dapat dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi o</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in yang te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdapat dalam bahan pangan, dimana pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ningkatan kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in dapat be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruh te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rhadap pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ningkatan daya se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rap air. Pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">miliki gugus karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ksil yang be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rsifat hidro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">filik, se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hingga se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in maka se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin banyak te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdapat gugus karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ksil yang dapat me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rap air se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin banyak. Pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nambahan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah yang se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin banyak me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">babkan kadar air biskuit se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ningkat, hal ini kare</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">na te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngandung pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in yang tinggi. Hal ini se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">jalan de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">litian Asfi </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">. (2017), dimana se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi rasio</span><span class="font0">l </span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan campuran pati sagu maka</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">kadar air </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> akan se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ningkat. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan hasil analisis bahan baku, te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">miliki kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 23,42%, se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">dangkan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 2,80%. Me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nurut Kahar </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al.</span><span class="font6"> (2022), pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdiri atas mo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kul dan asam-asam amino</span><span class="font0">l </span><span class="font6">yang dapat me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngikat air dalam pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">duk biskuit se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hingga me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngakibatkan se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin sulit suatu bahan untuk me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pas air se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">lama pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">manasan. Kadar air pada biskuit dapat me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">njadi salah satu parame</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">r pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nting yang dapat me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi masa simpan suatu bahan maupun pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">duk pangan. Kadar air biskuit me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngacu pada syarat mutu biskuit SNI 2973:2018 yaitu maksimal 5%. Hal ini be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rarti pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah pada se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mua pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nghasilkan biskuit de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan kadar air yang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nuhi standar.</span></p>
<h2><a name="bookmark25"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark26"></a>Kadar Abu</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">cara prage</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">latinisasi dan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruh tidak nyata (P&gt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rhadap kadar abu biskuit. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 2 dapat dilihat bahwa kadar abu biskuit be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 3,58% sampai de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan 3,96%. Se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin banyak pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nggunaan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbuatan biskuit tidak me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngakibatkan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ningkatan yang signifikan pada kadar abu dari biskuit. Hal te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">but dapat dise</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">babkan kare</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">na kandungan kadar abu yang te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rkandung pada bahan baku yang juga tidak</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">da jauh. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 1 dapat dilihat bahwa nilai kadar abu pada te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 2,98% dan kadar abu pada te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 3,95%. Se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">lain itu, adanya pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nambahan bahan pendukung yang digunakan dalam pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbuatan biskuit juga diduga dapat be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruh te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rhadap kadar abu. Me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nurut Irmawati </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al.</span><span class="font6"> (2014), kadar abu biskuit juga dapat dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi o</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h bahan pendukung pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbuat ado</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nan biskuit se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rti </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">baking po</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">wde</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">r</span><span class="font6">. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sarnya kadar abu me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sarnya kandungan mine</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ral yang te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdapat dalam suatu bahan. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l Ko</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mpo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sisi Bahan Pangan Dire</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kto</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rat Gizi Masyarakat (2017), mine</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ral yang te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rkandung pada te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu dalam 100 gr bahan yaitu kalium (940,0 mg), kalsium (89 mg), fo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sfo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">r (125 mg), be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">si (3,9), natrium (42 mg), te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbaga (0,80 mg), se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ng (0,6 mg) se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">dangkan pada kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngandung be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rapa mine</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ral se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rti kalsium (293 mg), fo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sfo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">r (134 mg), be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">si (3,7 mg), natrium (7 mg), kalium (360,7 mg), te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbaga (0,34 mg) se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rta se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ng (1,4 mg).</span></p>
<h2><a name="bookmark27"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark28"></a>Kadar Protein</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">cara prage</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">latinisasi dan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rhadap kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in biskuit. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 2 dapat dilihat bahwa kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in biskuit be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 3,11% sampai 8,13%. Kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h pada P0 (100:0) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 3,11% dan nilai kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h pada P5 (50:50) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 8,13%. Kandungan pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in dalam biskuit dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi o</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h bahan baku yang digunakan. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 1 dapat dilihat bahwa kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in pada te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 23,42% le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">bih tinggi dibandingkan kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 2,80%. Hal te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">but me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin banyak pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nambahan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbuatan biskuit mampu me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rikan sumbangan pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in yang tinggi te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rhadap te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hingga mampu me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nghasilkan biskuit de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in yang se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi. Hal ini se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">jalan de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">litian So</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">e</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">paryo</span><span class="font0">l </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al.</span><span class="font6"> (2018), yang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nyatakan bahwa se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nambahan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbuatan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">fo</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">o</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">d bar</span><span class="font6"> maka se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">fo</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">o</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">d bar</span><span class="font6"> yang dihasilkan. Me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nurut Widiantara </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">. (2018), kandungan pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in yang te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rkandung dalam pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">duk co</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">o</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kie</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">s juga dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi o</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h ko</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mpo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sisi bahan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nyusun se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rti susu bubuk dan kuning te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">lur. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan SNI 2973:2018, kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in minimal untuk biskuit adalah 4,5%. Jika dibandingkan de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rsyaratan kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in minimal pada SNI, dapat dikatakan bahwa kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in biskuit yang dihasilkan pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P0 dan P1 tidak me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nuhi</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rsyaratan mutu SNI biskuit se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">dangkan kadar pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P2, P3, P4 dan P5 sudah me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nuhi pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rsyaratan mutu SNI biskuit.</span></p>
<h2><a name="bookmark29"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark30"></a>Kadar Lemak</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">cara prage</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">latinisasi dan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rhadap kadar le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mak biskuit. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 2 dapat dilihat bahwa kadar le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mak biskuit be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 27,97% sampai 30,01%. Kadar le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mak te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P0 (100:0) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 27,97% yang tidak be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">da nyata de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P1 (90:10) se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 28,76%, se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">dangkan nilai kadar le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mak te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h pada P5 (50:50) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 30,01% yang tidak be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">da nyata de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P4 (60:40) dan P3 (70:30) yaitu masing-masing se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 29,82% dan 29,29%. Kandungan le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mak te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">but dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h dari bahan baku yang digunakan pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbuatan biskuit yaitu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah. Adanya pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">daan kandungan le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mak dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi o</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h jumlah pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nambahan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah yang digunakan pada se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">tiap pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan. Se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">iring de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rtambahnya rasio</span><span class="font0">l </span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah yang digunakan maka kadar le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mak yang te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdapat dalam biskuit yang dihasilkan se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ningkat.</span></p>

Nilai rata-rata yang diikuti o</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h huruf yang be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">da pada ko</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">lo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">m yang sama me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">da nyata (P&lt;0,05)</span></p>

Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 1 dapat dilihat bahwa kadar le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mak te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 5,92% dan kadar le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mak te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 2,37%.</span></p>
<h2><a name="bookmark31"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark32"></a>Kadar Karbohidrat</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngujian kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat dilakukan de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">to</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">de</span><span class="font0">l </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">by diffe</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">re</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">nce</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6">. Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">cara prage</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">latinisasi dan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rhadap kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat biskuit. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 2 dapat dilihat bahwa kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat biskuit be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 54,37% sampai de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan 62,73%. Kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat biskuit te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P0 (100:0) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 62,73%, se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">dangkan nilai kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat biskuit te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdapat pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P5 (50:50) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 54,37%.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Hal ini dapat disimpulkan bahwa se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi rasio</span><span class="font0">l </span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi maka kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat pada biskuit akan se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi. Se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">baliknya se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi rasio</span><span class="font0">l </span><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nambahan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah maka kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat pada biskuit se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sarnya kandungan karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat pada biskuit dihitung se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">cara </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">by diffe</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">re</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">nc</span><span class="font6">e</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">, dimana kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat yang dihasilkan dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi o</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h ko</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mpo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">n nutrisi lain se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rti kadar air, abu, le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mak dan pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">in. Se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi kandungan nutrisi yang lain maka kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat yang dihasilkan akan se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah, se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">baliknya se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah kandungan nutrisi yang lain maka se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat yang dihasilkan. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan hasil analisis bahan baku yang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">miliki nilai kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat tinggi yaitu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdapat pada te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi, se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hingga se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin banyak pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nggunaan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi maka se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat biskuit yang dihasilkan. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 1 dapat dilihat bahwa kadar karbo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hidrat te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 85,75% le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">bih tinggi dibandingkan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 57,34%.</span></p>
<h2><a name="bookmark33"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark34"></a>Hasil Analisis Karakteristik Fisik Uji Tekstur (</span><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Hardness</span><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;">)</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Hasil analisis uji te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kstur biskuit yang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">liputi </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">hardne</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6"> (ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan) dapat dilihat pada Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 3. Analisis te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kstur pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">litian ini dilakukan untuk me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nge</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">tahui tingkat ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">duk biskuit yang dihasilkan. Nilai ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi nilai yang dihasilkan maka pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">duk te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">but se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ras, hal ini te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rjadi kare</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">na se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin besar gaya atau te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kanan yang dibutuhkan untuk me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nusuk atau me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nghancurkan pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">duk te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">but. Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">cara prage</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">latinisasi dan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rhadap ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan (</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">hardne</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6">) biskuit. Be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">l 3 me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan biskuit be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 10,20 N sampai de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan 19,52 N. Nilai ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P0 (100:0) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 10,20 N yang tidak be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">da nyata de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P1 (90:10) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 11,64 N, se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">dangkan nilai ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rtinggi te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rdapat pada pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P5 (50:50) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 19,52 N yang tidak be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">da nyata de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rlakuan P4 (60:40) yaitu se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sar 17,63 N. Se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin banyak pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nggunaan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi maka se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan biskuit, se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">baliknya se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin banyak pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nambahan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rah maka se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi nilai ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan biskuit.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Tingkat ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan pada pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">duk biskuit be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rkaitan de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan sifat ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nyahan (Aini dan Wirawani, 2013). Se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi tingkat ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rasan maka ke</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nyahan biskuit se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ndah. Pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nambahan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi yang se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin banyak me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nghasilkan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kstur biskuit yang re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nyah dan mudah hancur di dalam mulut. Hal ini se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">jalan de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">litian Kahar </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">. (2022), dimana se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nambahan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar kuning te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rmo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nghasilkan biskuit de</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kstur yang padat, le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbut dan re</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nyah di dalam mulut. Hal te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">but dapat dipe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi o</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">h kandungan pati pada te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pung ubi jalar ungu hasil mo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">difikasi prage</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">latinisasi, dimana granula pati te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">lah dirusak se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">lama pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">s pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">manasan se</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">hingga granula pati akan me</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">nge</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">mbang kare</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">na mo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kul-mo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kul air akan be</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">trasi masuk ke</span><span class="font0">l </span><span class="font6">dalam granula pati dan te</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">rangkap pada susunan mo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kul-mo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">le</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">kul amilo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">sa dan amilo</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ktin. Terjadinya peningkatan ukuran partikel pati yang semakin besar menyebabkan air mudah menyerap dan pada saat pro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ses pemanggangan air akan menguap sehingga terbentuk ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngga-ro</span><span class="font0">l</span><span class="font6">ngga yang menyebabkan tekstur biskuit menjadi renyah.</span></p>
